   <script type="text/javascript">
    var Wwidth = $(window).width(),
                 Wheight = $(window).height(),
                 iwight = window.innerWidth,
                 iheight = window.innerHeight;
     
             if(bIsIphoneOs || bIsMidp || bIsUc7 || bIsUc || bIsAndroid || bIsCE || bIsWM){
                 $('#kvArea').find('.kvpc').remove();   
             }else{
                 $('#kvArea').find('.kvmobile').remove();
             } 
             var Wwidth = $(window).width(),
                 Wheight = $(window).height(); 
             var kkp = $('#kvArea .swiper-slide');
             var supjson = [];
              
             for (var a=0;a<kkp.length;a++) {
                  supjson.push(a);
             };
              
             supjson.splice(0,2)
          
              
             var Snum = Math.floor((Math.random()*supjson.length)); 
             supjson.splice(Snum,1);
             for(i in supjson){
                 $('#kvArea .swiper-slide').eq(supjson[i]).addClass('rme');
                 $('.NavTabArea a.tabs_a').eq(supjson[i]).addClass('rme');                           
             }
             $('.rme').remove();
             $('#kvArea .tabs').show();
 
             //KV position
             function kvpos(wordW,wordH){
                 if(bIsIphoneOs || bIsMidp || bIsUc7 || bIsUc || bIsAndroid || bIsCE || bIsWM){
                     //上
                     $('.mobile .mpos1').css({'width':'520px','margin-top':'100px'});
                     //中
                     $('.mobile .mpos2').css({'width':'520px','margin-top':'375px'});
                     //下
                     $('.mobile .mpos3').css({'width':'520px','margin-top':'650px'});  
                 }else{
                     //左中   
                     $('.pos1').css({
                         'margin-top':-wordH/2,
                         'margin-left':-wordW/2-0.3*Wwidth
                     })
                     //中中
                     $('.pos2').css({
                         'margin-top':-wordH/2,
                         'margin-left':-wordW/2
                     })
                     //右中
                     $('.pos3').css({
                         'margin-top':-wordH/2,
                         'margin-right':-wordW/2-0.3*Wwidth
                     })
                     //左上中   
                     $('.pos4').css({
                         'margin-top':-wordH/2-0.22*Wheight,
                         'margin-left':-wordW/2-0.3*Wwidth
                     })
                     //右上中  
                     $('.pos5').css({
                         'margin-top':-wordH/2-0.22*Wheight,
                         'margin-right':-wordW/2-0.3*Wwidth
                     })
                     //上中  
                     $('.pos6').css({
                         'margin-top':-wordH/2-0.22*Wheight,
                         'margin-left':-wordW/2
                     })
                 }
             }  
         $(document).ready(function(){        
             //kv轮播
 
             function videomethod(){
                 $('.videoFlash').remove();
                 if($('#kvArea .swiper-slide-active').hasClass('videoblock')){
                     var $videopos = $('#kvArea .swiper-slide-active.videoblock').find('a.MainArea');
                     var videourl1='/images/Bravia1920x1080.mp4';
                     var videourl2='/images/kv_spxb60.mp4';
                     var videourl3='/images/sds22.mp4';
                     var eqvideo = tabsSwiper.activeLoopIndex;
                     var ksheight = $('#kvArea .swiper-container').height();
                     $videopos.html(' ');
                     if(!+[1,]){
                         //IE浏览器
                         var flash_player1 = $('<div class="videoPlayerFlash1 videoFlash"></div>');
                         var flash_player2 = $('<div class="videoPlayerFlash2 videoFlash"></div>');
                         var flash_player3 = $('<div class="videoPlayerFlash3 videoFlash"></div>');
                         function ievideo(videoorder,videofile){
                             $(videoorder).html('').flash({
                                 'src':'/images/player.swf',
                                 'width':Wwidth,
                                 'height':ksheight,
                                 'allowfullscreen':'true',
                                 'wmode':'transparent',
                                 'loop':'true',
                                 'flashvars':{
                                     backcolor:'#DDDDDDD',
                                     frontcolor:'#000000',
                                     autostart:'true',
                                     allowfullscreen:'true',
                                     width:Wwidth,
                                     height:ksheight,
                                     file:videofile
                                 }
                             },
                                 { version: 7 }
                             );
                         }
                          
                         $('.videoFlash').css({
                             'width':Wwidth,
                             'height':ksheight,
                             'margin':'0 auto'
                         });
                         switch (eqvideo){
                             case 0:
                                 ievideo(flash_player1,videourl1)
                                 $(flash_player1).appendTo($videopos);
                                 break;
                             case 1:
                                 ievideo(flash_player2,videourl2)
                                 $(flash_player2).appendTo($videopos);
                                 break;
                             case 2:
                                 ievideo(flash_player3,videourl3)
                                 $(flash_player3).appendTo($videopos);
                                 break; 
                         }
                     }else{
                         //非IE浏览器
                         var videoinfo1 = 'videoPlayerFlash1';
                         var videoinfo2 = 'videoPlayerFlash2';
                         var videoinfo3 = 'videoPlayerFlash3';  
                         function kvideo(videoorder,videofile){
                             $('<video class="'+videoorder+' videoFlash" width="100%" height="auto" preload="auto" autoplay loop><source src="'+videofile+'" type="video/mp4"></video>').appendTo($videopos);
                         }
                          
                         switch (eqvideo){
                             case 0:
                                 kvideo(videoinfo1,videourl1)
                                 break;
                             case 1:
                                 kvideo(videoinfo2,videourl2)
                                 break;
                             case 2:
                                 kvideo(videoinfo3,videourl3)
                                 break;
                         }
                          
                         if(bIsIphoneOs || bIsMidp || bIsUc7 || bIsUc || bIsAndroid || bIsCE || bIsWM){
                             $('.videoFlash').css({
                                 'width':'100%',
                                 'height':'auto',
                                 'margin-top':'32%'
                             })
                            
                         }
                     }
                 }else{
                     $('.videoFlash').remove();
                 }
              
                 if($('#kvArea .swiper-slide').hasClass('swiper-slide-active')){
                     if($('#kvArea .swiper-slide-active').hasClass('videoblock')){
                     }else{   
                         var mke = $('#kvArea .swiper-slide-active');   
                         var wordW = mke.find('.KvWord').outerWidth();
                         var wordH = mke.find('.KvWord').outerHeight();
                         kvpos(wordW,wordH);
                         setTimeout(function(){
                             $('#kvArea .swiper-slide .KvWord').fadeIn(100).addClass('fadeInUp')
                         },600)
                     }
                 } 
             } 
 
 
 
 
             var tabsSwiper = new Swiper('#kvArea .swiper-container',{
                 loop:true,
                 autoplay : 5000,
                 speed:800,
                 onSwiperCreated: function(){
                     $('.videoblock').css({'background':'#000'});
                 },
                 onSlideChangeStart: function(){
                   $(".tabs .active").removeClass('active');
                   $(".tabs a").eq(tabsSwiper.activeLoopIndex).addClass('active'); 
                   $('.swiper-slide .KvWord').removeClass('fadeInUp').hide();
                 },
                 onSlideChangeEnd: function(){
                     videomethod()
                 }
             })
 
             first();
             function first(){
                 var mke = $('#kvArea .swiper-slide-active');
                 if(mke.hasClass('videoblock')){
                    videomethod()        
                 }else{
                     var wordW = mke.find('.KvWord').outerWidth();
                     var wordH = mke.find('.KvWord').outerHeight();
                     kvpos(wordW,wordH);
                     mke.find('.KvWord').fadeIn(100).addClass('fadeInUp') 
                     return false
                 }
             }
 
             $('#kvArea .arrow-left').bind('click', function(e){
                e.preventDefault()
                tabsSwiper.swipePrev()
             })
             $('#kvArea .arrow-right').bind('click', function(e){
                e.preventDefault()
                tabsSwiper.swipeNext()
             })   
             $(".tabs a").bind('touchstart mousedown',function(e){
                e.preventDefault()
                $(".tabs .active").removeClass('active')
                $(this).addClass('active');  
                tabsSwiper.swipeTo($(this).index())
             })
             $(".tabs a").click(function(e){
                 e.preventDefault();
             })
             
             $('.swiper-slide .KvWord').addClass('fadeInUp');
 
             $('#kvArea').hover(function(){
                 tabsSwiper.stopAutoplay();
             },function(){
                 tabsSwiper.startAutoplay();
             })
            
             $('#kvArea .swiper-wrapper').find('a').each(function(index,item){
                 $(this).bind('click',function(){
                     var el = $(this);
                     var aveq = tabsSwiper.activeLoopIndex;
                     var elh3 = $('.NavTabArea a.tabs_a').eq(aveq).find('h3.TabWord').html();
                     aveq = aveq + 1;
                     var t_trace = 'KV'+':第'+ aveq +'帧:'+':'+elh3;
                     trace_method(el,t_trace) 
                 })
             })
              
             //最近活动
             var mySwiper = new Swiper('#ActiveKvArea .swiper-container2',{
                 pagination: '.pagination',
                 loop:true,
                 grabCursor: true,
                 paginationClickable: true,
                 speed:800,
                 autoplay : 5000
             })
             $('.Active_main .arrow-left').bind('click', function(e){
                 e.preventDefault()
                 mySwiper.swipePrev()
             })
             $('.Active_main .arrow-right').bind('click', function(e){
                 e.preventDefault()
                 mySwiper.swipeNext()
             })
             $('#ActiveKvArea .swiper-wrapper').find('a').each(function(index,item){
                 $(this).bind('click',function(){
                     var el = $(this);
                     var imgp = "";
                     if(el.hasClass('mrt15')){
                         imgp="左边";
                     }else{
                         imgp="右边";
                     }
                     var aveq = mySwiper.activeLoopIndex;
                     aveq = aveq + 1;
                     var imgname = $(this).find('img').attr('alt');
                     var t_trace = 'Recent Activity'+':第'+aveq+'帧'+imgp+':'+':'+imgname;
                     trace_method(el,t_trace)
                      
                 })
             })             
             function trace_method(val,val2){
                 if(val.hasClass('out')){
                     var s=s_gi('sonycnstyle');
                     s.tl(this,'o', val2);
                 }else{
                     $.cookie('tracecode',val2);
                 }
             }
         })
   </script>
